! Title: ðŸ¦¨ Anti-Pepe List
! Version: 27February2023v1
! Expires: 4 days
! Description:  Pepe the Frog, while beloved by many internet memers, has also become the go-to symbol of many horrendous alt-right movements, culminating in Frenworld and Clown World. If you're worried that people who use him do not have the best intentions, this is how to avoid both him and them.
! Note: Due to me (The list maintainer) running into mental health problems after looking through heaps of horrendous "artpieces", my lists can no longer deal with deviantART or Inkbunny.
! Note 2: (Un)fortunately, this is not about the Real Madrid player called Pepe, even if he does dive like he was acting in a Saving Private Ryan theater play, and that I hate him for it.
! Note 3: After the amount of blocked emotes reached into the quad-digits, Twitch's video feeds would quite frequently stutter and freeze for me, even on an Intel i5-4460 desktop. Thus it was no longer feasible to remove blocked-emote-using comments entirely. Sure I was also using Folding@Home at the time of the stuttering, which took up 85% of my CPU power, but still.
! Homepage: https://github.com/DandelionSprout/adfilt/blob/master/Wiki/General-info.md#-english
